	}
}
country_event = {
	id = wallace.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event wallace.2" }
	title = wallace.2.t
	desc = wallace.2.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = wallace.2.a

		hidden_effect = {
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = USA_WAL_64_CRA
				keep_completed = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The NYT Report on the massacre
	id = wallace.impeachment.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event wallace.impeachment.1" }
	title = wallace.impeachment.1.t
	desc = wallace.impeachment.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_family_tv

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Damn the Media
		name = wallace.impeachment.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		country_event = {
			id = wallace.impeachment.2
			days = 1
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_political_power = -50
		set_variable = { USA_wallace_impeachment_support = 10 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_wallace_impeachment_support = WAL_SEGREGATION }
		custom_effect_tooltip = wallace.impeachment.support.introduction.tt
	}
}

}

	}
}

country_event = { #Do we launch it, or put it on the backburner for a better moment? (we might not get a second chance)
	id = wallace.impeachment.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event wallace.impeachment.5" }
	title = wallace.impeachment.5.t
	desc = wallace.impeachment.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #LAUNCH IT NOW
		name = wallace.impeachment.5.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_plead_unity
			}
			country_event = {
				id = wallace.impeachment.6
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_deny_responsibility
			}
			country_event = {
				id = wallace.impeachment.26
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_go_nixon
			}
			country_event = {
				id = wallace.impeachment.27
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Maybe we should wait for a few more facts?
		name = wallace.impeachment.5.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		country_event = {
			id = wallace.impeachment.11
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { new_bill_support = 2 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = new_bill_support
					min = 0
					max = NPP_C_senators
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = NPP_C_supporting_senators
					min = 0
					max = NPP_C_senators
				}
				add_to_variable = { supporting_senators = new_bill_support }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = wallace.617 #SS passes
	title = wallace.617.t
	desc = wallace.617.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_rdc_generic_2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = wallace.617.a #well love you too
		tno_pensions_improve = yes
		set_variable = { tno_pensions_effectiveness = 50 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = wallace_617_tt
		social_funding_minimal_increase_low = yes

		set_temp_variable = { misc_costs_temp = 0.2 } #starting cost
		set_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = 0.05 } #direct transfer spending leads to more money in circulation

		hidden_effect = { #generic effect
			if = { #no segregation, less poverty
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_WAL_segregated_SS
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = WAL_passed_not_racist_SS
				TNO_improve_poverty_low = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rural_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_rural_nat = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rural_nat_shift
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_nat = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_nat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_nat_shift
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_nat = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_nat_shift
		}
		if = { #segregation
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_WAL_segregated_SS
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { tno_health_care_effectiveness = 20 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAL_segregated_SS_passed_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_nativists_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_nativists_nat = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_nativists_nat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_nativists_nat_shift
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_dem = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_dem }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_dem_shift

			add_to_variable = { WAL_SEGREGATION = 2 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_TT_WAL_SEG_LOW_more_seg_med_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = USA_wal64_spend_spend_spend
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = 0.05 } #more spending = more inflation
			social_funding_maximal_increase_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_wal64_spend_spend_spend_passed_tt

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rural_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_rural_nat = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rural_nat_shift

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_nat = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_nat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_nat_shift

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_voters_header_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_nat = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_nat_shift

			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { tno_health_care_effectiveness = 10 }
				TNO_improve_poverty_low = yes
				add_to_temp_variable = { misc_costs = 0.1 }
			}
		}
		TNO_update_policy_effectiveness = yes
		econ_inflation_change = yes #tot depends on if you passed spend, spend, spend or not

		custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_econ_misc_costs_increase_tt
		hidden_effect = { #cost spirit
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_WAL_SS_and_healthcare_dynmod }
				}
				set_variable = { USA_WAL_SS_and_healthcare_misc_costs = misc_costs_temp }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { USA_WAL_SS_and_healthcare_misc_costs = misc_costs_temp }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_WAL_SS_and_healthcare_dynmod }
			}
		}
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event chase.pol.5" }
	title = chase.pol.5.t
	desc = chase.pol.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_presidential_podium

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_mcs_68_start_party_crisis
			add_to_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			USA_reload_presidential_tree = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Add fail condition once that is in
		name = chase.pol.5.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_mcs_68_npp_shattered
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { mcs_left_satisfaction_change = -0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { mcs_center_satisfaction_change = -0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { mcs_right_satisfaction_change = -0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { mcs_south_satisfaction_change = -0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { mcs_fascist_satisfaction_change = -0.25 }
		mcs_unity_check = yes
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event chase.rog.5" }
	title = chase.rog.5.t
	desc = chase.rog.5.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

		name = chase.rog.5.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_mcs_68_anger_right
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_mcs_68_anger_southern
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_mcs_68_anger_center
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_mcs_68_rog_start
		add_ideas = USA_mcs_revolt_of_the_generals_stage_1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = revolt_of_the_generals_active
			clr_country_flag = mcs_revolt_prelude_2
			clr_country_flag = mcs_revolt_prelude_3
			clr_country_flag = mcs_revolt_prelude_4

			add_to_variable = { mcs_south_satisfaction_change = -0.08 } #Not a good look for these people either
			add_to_variable = { mcs_center_satisfaction_change = -0.06 } #Still pretty disapointed in you but military stuff is not their primary concern
			set_variable = { mcs_divisiveness = 10 }
			mcs_influence_calculation = yes
			mcs_unity_check = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = revolt_of_the_generals_active }
				country_event = {
					id = chase.rog.7
					days = 7
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_rural_dem = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_dem }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_dem }

country_event = { #Did Stennis exceed his authority?
	id = chase.rog.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event chase.rog.8" }
	title = chase.rog.8.t
	desc = chase.rog.8.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_country_flag = revolt_of_the_generals_active }
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = chase.rog.8.a
		trigger = {
			has_political_power > 24.99
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = chase.rog.8
				days = 33
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = chase.rog.8.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_NPP_unity
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_mcs_68_rog_lose_face
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = chase.rog.9
				days = 33
			}
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_rural_rep = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_rep }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_rep }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_rep }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_rep }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_rep }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_rep }

			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_nat }
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_rural_pro = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
			if = { #Unfuck the army
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = USA_mcs_revolt_of_the_generals_stage_2
						has_idea = USA_mcs_revolt_of_the_generals_stage_3
						has_idea = USA_mcs_revolt_of_the_generals_stage_4
						has_idea = USA_mcs_revolt_of_the_generals_stage_5
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = chase.rog.42 days = 365 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = USA_mcs_revolt_of_the_generals_stage_1 }
				country_event = { id = chase.rog.45 days = 365 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			add_ideas = USA_Sid_McMath_hog

		}
	}

country_event = { #shhh hidden
	id = chase.crisis.party.17
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event chase.crisis.party.17" }
	title = chase.crisis.party.17.t
	desc = chase.crisis.party.17.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_npp_generic_2
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = chase.crisis.party.17.a #Sounds goods
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MCS_South_Worked_With }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = 10 }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_supporting_senators = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_LNPP_support = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_CNPP_support = 10 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_CNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_LNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_L_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_C_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_L_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_L_senators
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_LNPP_support }
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_CNPP_support }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MCS_Centre_Worked_With }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_supporting_senators = 10 }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_Y_supporting_senators = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_FRNPP_support = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_YNPP_support = 10 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_FRNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_YNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_Y_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_Y_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_Y_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_FR_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_FRNPP_support }
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_YNPP_support }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MCS_Left_Worked_With }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_supporting_senators = 10 }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_Y_supporting_senators = 10 }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_FRNPP_support = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_YNPP_support = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_CNPP_support = 5 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_FRNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_YNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_Y_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_CNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_Y_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_Y_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_FR_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_C_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_FRNPP_support }
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_YNPP_support }
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_CNPP_support }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MCS_Yockey_Worked_With }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = 10 }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_supporting_senators = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_LNPP_support = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_CNPP_support = 10 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_CNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_LNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_L_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_Y_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_Y_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_FR_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_L_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_L_senators
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_LNPP_support }
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_CNPP_support }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MCS_South_Worked_With }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = 10 }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_supporting_senators = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_LNPP_support = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_CNPP_support = 10 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_CNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_LNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_L_senators
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_LNPP_support }
			subtract_from_variable = { supporting_senators = new_CNPP_support }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MCS_mid_support }
			add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_supporting_senators = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_LNPP_support = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_CNPP_support = 10 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_CNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_LNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_C_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_FR_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			add_to_variable = { supporting_senators = new_LNPP_support }
			add_to_variable = { supporting_senators = new_CNPP_support }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MCS_high_support }
			add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_supporting_senators = 20 }
			add_to_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_LNPP_support = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { new_CNPP_support = 20 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_CNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = new_LNPP_support
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_C_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_FR_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}
			add_to_variable = { supporting_senators = new_LNPP_support }
			add_to_variable = { supporting_senators = new_CNPP_support }
		}
	}
}
